## https://github.com/OSPrantoTech/BDIX-Server-Checker/blob/main/ftp_servers(Optional).json

```json
[
  {
    "name": "FTP Server 10.1.1.1",
    "url": "http://10.1.1.1"
  },
  {
    "name": "Data Server 10.1.1.1",
    "url": "http://10.1.1.1/Data"
  },
```
